  <script>
   function setUseMobileSiteCookie(useMobile) {
					const value = useMobile ? 'yes' : 'no'
					const date = new Date()
					const maxAge = 365 * 24 * 60 * 60
					date.setTime(date.getTime() + maxAge * 1000)
					const expires = '; expires=' + date.toUTCString()
					const cookieValuePair = 'useMobileSite=' + value
					document.cookie = cookieValuePair + expires + '; path=/; maxAge=' + maxAge

					if (document.cookie.includes(cookieValuePair)) {
						window.location.reload(true)
					} else {
						console.error('Failed to set useMobileSite cookie.')
					}
				}

				/*
				 * If ?fromApp=true, it's possible for user is already in the correct mode, so only try
				 * reloading if that's the case. In fact, trying to reload the page regardless causes an 
				 * infinite loop as the ?fromApp=true parameter is always present.
				 */
				const isMobileWidth = screen.width < 768
				if (isMobileWidth && !document.cookie.includes('useMobileSite=yes')) {
					setUseMobileSiteCookie(true)
				} else if (!isMobileWidth && !document.cookie.includes('useMobileSite=no')) {
					setUseMobileSiteCookie(false)
				}
  </script>

       <section class="production-synopsis">
        <div class="review body-text -prose -hero prettify">
         <h3 class="hidden">
          Synopsis
         </h3>
         <h4 class="tagline">
          In 28 days it began. In 28 weeks it spread. In 28 years it evolved.
         </h4>
         <div class="truncate" data-truncate="450">
          <p>
           Twenty-eight years since the rage virus escaped a biological weapons laboratory, now, still in a ruthlessly enforced quarantine, some have found ways to exist amidst the infected. One such group lives on a small island connected to the mainland by a single, heavily-defended causeway. When one member departs on a mission into the dark heart of the mainland, he discovers secrets, wonders, and horrors that have mutated not only the infected but other survivors as well.
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>

               <p>
                the children i teach each and every week were all born between october 2019 and march 2020. they spent their first year of life isolated from the rest of the world as a result of a nearly unprecedented pandemic that completely upended every aspect of modern society. said world they’ve grown up in since is radically different from the one any of us knew as children - one they’ll never have any knowledge of. and though most are only a few months away from six, as soon as they start kindergarten in the fall, the world as it is now will start to force them to age faster and faster, unfairly robbing them of the rest of their youth.

          <article class="production-viewing -viewing js-production-viewing" data-person="emmasaurustex" data-viewing-id="919790810">
           <a class="avatar -a40" href="/emmasaurustex/">
            <img alt="~ Em ~" height="40" src="https://a.ltrbxd.com/resized/avatar/upload/6/8/9/3/6/4/7/shard/avtr-0-80-0-80-crop.jpg?v=3bc2a0e7b2" width="40"/>
           </a>
           <div class="body">
            <div class="attribution-block -large">
             <div class="body">
              <span class="attribution-detail">
               <a class="context" href="/emmasaurustex/film/28-years-later/" title="Read ~ Em ~’s review">
                Review by
                <span class="owner">
                 <strong class="displayname">
                  ~ Em ~
                 </strong>
                </span>
               </a>
              </span>
              <span class="content-reactions-strip -viewing">
               <span class="rating -green rated-4">
                ★★
               </span>
               <a class="inlineicon icon-16 -ignoreactionpseudo icon-comment" href="/emmasaurustex/film/28-years-later/#comments">
                <span class="icon" role="presentation">
                </span>
                <span class="label">
                 13
                </span>
               </a>
              </span>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="js-review">
             <div class="body-text -prose -reset js-review-body js-collapsible-text" data-full-text-url="/s/full-text/viewing:919790810/" data-is-translatable="true" lang="en">
              <div class="collapsed-text">
               <p>
                I wanted to love it, I really did, but 28 Years Later is one of the biggest disappointments of the year.
               </p>
               <p>
                The trailer is highly misleading. It makes the film look like a gritty horror film, which it isn't. Instead, it plays out more like a family drama with some horror scenes here and there, which feel quite random compared to the rest of the story.
               </p>
               <p>
                There are also some really odd editing choices, random scenes, and ill-fitting musical choices. It feels like the filmmakers didn't know what to do in terms of a story, so they threw together a few random plot points. It’s a bit all over the place and feels disjointed.
               </p>
               <p>
                I also didn't care about the…
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>
